@017 ZHING BSDAD YOD PA DANG 'PHRAD, GZUGS BYAD LTA BAS CHOG MI

LO'I ZLA 3 TSES 15 NYIN RGYA NAG PHYOGS SU CHIBS KHA BSGYUR, LAM BAR

RGYA SOG BOD RIGS KYI DPON 'BANGS DANG, RGYA DANG MAN JU'I

BLON CHEN DMAG DPUNG BCAS KYIS PHEBS BSU DANG DNGOS 'BUL

RGYA CHE BA MDZAD,

CHU SBRUL (1653) LO'I ZLA BA DANG BOR GONG MA HRUN KRI DANG

MJAL 'PHRAD BYUNG, MJAL DAR RTZE SPROD GNANG, SLAR ZLA

GNYIS PAR GONG MA'I PHO BRANG DU GDAN DRANGS NAS DNGOS 'BUL

GTOS CHE BA PHUL BA SOGS MJAL 'PHRAD THENGS KHA SHAS GNANG,

GONG MA DANG SOG PO'I SBYIN BDAG RNAMS KYIS GSOL BA BTAB PA

BZHIN RGYA NAG DANG, SOG YUL GYI DGON SDE RNAMS LA BCA' YIG

DANG BKA' SLOB SOGS STZAL, DE NAS ZHI DRAG GI BLON CHEN

RNAMS KYIS PHEBS SKYEL DANG BCAS ZLA PA GNYIS PA'I TSES NYI SHU'I

NYIN PE CIN NAS CHIBS KHA BSGYUR, ZLA BA LNGA BA'I TSES LNGA'I NYIN

TA'I KHA ZHES PA'I SA GNAS SU PHEBS SKABS, SHIN TU RGYA CHE BA'I

MDZAD SGO'I THOG GONG MA'I DMIGS BSAL GYI MI SNAS GSER GYI

THAM GA DANG, GSER GYI GLEGS BU BCO LNGA LA MIG DANG 'BREL

@179 NAS LTEB CHOG PA'I NANG, MAN JU, HOR, BOD YIG 'BUR

DOD DU BRKOS PA'I NANG, NUB KYI LHA GNAS CHES DGE BA BDE

BAR GNAS PA'I SANGS RGYAS KYI BKA' LUNG GNAM 'OG GI SKYE 'GRO

THAMS CAD BSTAN PA GCIG TU GYUR PA 'GYUR MED RDO RJE 'CHANG RGYA

MTSO'I BLA MA ZHES MTSAN BSTOD PHUL, T'A LA'I BLA MA RIN PO CHE

NAS KYANG GONG DANG 'DRA BA'I GSER GYI GLEGS BU'I THOG BOD,

MAN, HOR GSUM GYI YI GE 'BUR DU DOD PA BRKOS PA'I NANG

GNAM GYI LHA 'JAM DBYANGS GONG MA BDAG PO CHEN PO ZHES MTSAN

BSTOD GONG MA'I MI SNA'I PHYAG TU PHUL, DE NAS MKHAR SNGON BRGYUD

ZI LING SKU 'BUM SOGS AA MDO'I DGON GNAS RNAMS DANG, MTSO

SNGON GYI SA GNAS KHAG CHAB MDO SOGS MDO STOD KYI DGON SDE

DANG, YUL SDE SOGS KYIS BSNYEN BKUR BLA NA MED PA ZHUS THOG

CHOS DANG ZANG ZING GI SBYIN PAS TSIM PAR BYAS TE, ZLA BA BCU

BA'I TSES NYER BZHI'I NYIN LHA LDAN DU 'BYOR 'DUG GO, ,

SHING RTA (1654) LO'I ZLA 12 TSES 7 NYIN GU SHR'I BSTAN

'DZIN CHOS RGYAL DGUNG GRANGS DON GNYIS THOG GZIM KHRI'I MTHA'

CAN DU GYUR,

SA KHYI (1658) LOR GU SHR'I HAN GYI SRAS BSTAN 'DZIN RDO RJE

LA RGYAL BO'I THOB GNANG, YAB KYI DUS LTAR SOG DMAG GI 'GO

@180 'DZIN MDZAD, LO DE'I ZLA GSUM PAR SDE SRID BSOD NAMS CHOS

'PHEL GSHEGS, LO GCIG LA GSANG RGYA MDZAD, LCAGS BYI

(1660) LO'I ZLA 7 TSES 13 NYIN JA'I SANG SDE BA ZER BA GRONG SMAD

'PHRIN LAS RGYA MTSOR SDE SRID KYI CHO LO GNANG BA DANG, DE DANG

MNYAM RGYAL BO BSTAN 'DZIN RDO RJE LA YANG, BSTAN 'DZIN D'A YAN

KH'ANG ZHES PA'I CHO LO STZAL TE, MCHOD YON GYIS MDZAD SGO DUS

GCIG LA GNANG, LCAGS GLANG (1661) LOR BAL BO'I DPUNG

DMAG GIS BOD KHONGS GLANG BU MKHAR DU TSUR RGOL BYUNG BAR BOD

DMAG GIS 'PHRAL DU SA MTSAMS NAS PHAR BSKRAD, CHU STAG

(1662) LOR PAn CHEN RIN PO CHE BLO BZANG CHOS KYI RGYAL MTSAN

SKU 'DAS GSUNGS 'DUG LO 'DIR 'BRAS RGYAL SRAS BSTAN SRUNG

RNAM RGYAL RGYAL SAR 'KHOD PA CHABS CIG T'A LA'I BLA MA RIN PO CHER

MJAL BAR LHA SAR PHEBS, SDE SRID KYANG MJAL TE KHRIMS YIG

ZHAL LCE BCU DRUG SKOR LA SLOB STON MANG BO ZHUS GNANG MDZAD,

SHING SBRUL (1665) LOR MAN JU GONG MA LNGA BA KHANG SHI RGYAL

BOS, DAL GEL DGE SLONG DANG, SHES RAB 'OD ZER GNYIS

DZA DRAG GIS MI SNAR MNGAGS TE T'A LA'I BLA MA RIN PO CHER ZHUS

DON, SOG PO TSOS RGYA'I SA MTSAMS BRGAL NAS RGYA GRONG RNAMS LA

RTAG TU GNOD PA BYED KYIN 'DUG PAS, RGYA SOG SA MTSAMS KYI

@181 DPON SDE RNAMS LA ZHAL TA BKA' SLOB GNANG MI SKU TSAB CHED

GTONG GNANG RGYU THUGS RJE CHE ZHES ZHUS PA LTAR, SA MTSAMS KYI

DPON SDE RNAMS LA, SA MTSAMS GTAN KHEL BA'I RANG SDE RANG

'DZIN DANG, SA MTSAMS BRGAL NAS RGYA SDE RNAMS LA BSUN

GTZER MI BYED PAR SNGAR LUGS LTAR TSONG 'BREL YAG PO BYAS NAS

'DUG DGOS, ZHES BKA' SLOB GNANG MKHAN BYAMS GLING MKHAN

PO TSUL KHRIMS RGYAL MTSAN DANG, KHANG GSAR RAB BRTAN PA

GTONG GNANG MDZAD PAS RTZOD GZHI ZHI 'JAGS DANG, 'BREL BA

SNGAR LUGS BZHIN YAG PO BYUNG,

ME LUG (1667) LOR PAn CHEN BLO BZANG YE SHES DPAL

BZANG BO, BKRA SHIS LHUN PO'I PHO BRANG RGYAL MTSAN MTHON POR SKU

GONG MA'I KHRIR BKOD, DE'I PHYI LOR SDE SRID GRONG SMAD PA 'PHRIN

LAS RGYA MTSO KHRI LO DGUR GNANG STE GSHEGS, DE RJES BSTAN

'DZIN D'A YAN RGYAL BO YANG 'DAS, SA SPREL (1668) LOR MON

PA AA LCOG PA'I STENG DU 'BRUG DMAG BYUNG BAR, AA LCOG PA'I RGYAB

GNYER LA BOD GZHUNG GI DMAG SONG NAS 'BRUG PA PHAM PAR BYAS

TE CHINGS BZHAG SHING YOS (1675) LOR MON 'BRUG GNYIS

'KHRUGS PA DANG, ME 'BRUG (1676) LOR 'BRUG PAS MON

DANG 'BRAS LJONGS LA BTZAN 'DZUL BYAS PAS, BOD GZHUNG GI

@182 DMAG SONG NAS 'BRAS LJONGS NAS 'BRUG DMAG PHYI 'PHUD BTANG,

SA CHA SHOR BA RNAMS PHYIR BLANGS, SA RTA (1678) LOR BOD

'BRUG BKA' MOL BYAS MOD CHINGS LEGS PO MA BYUNG, SA BYA

(1669) LOR MCHOD DPON BLO BZANG MTHU STOBS SDE SRID DU

BSKO GZHAG GNANG, 'DI LA ZANGS RI BLO BZANG MTHU STOBS YANG

ZER, DE'I PHYI LOR AO ROD KYI NANG DU SDE GZAR LANGS PAR, RGYAL

DBANG DANG SDE SRID KYIS GANGS CAN MKHAN PO DKON MCHOG RIN

CHEN MNGAGS TE PHAN TSUN LUGS LEGS BYUNG,

LCAGS PHAG (1671) LOR PAn CHEN BLO BZANG YE SHES RGYAL

DBANG MCHOG LA DGE TSUL GYI SDOM PA ZHU BA, MDO SNGAGS KYI CHOS

MANG BO ZHU BA'I DON DU LHA SAR PHEBS, GU SHR'I HAN GYI SRAS CHUNG BA

DKON MCHOG DA LA'I LA BSTAN 'DZIN DA LA'I CHO LO DANG BCAS

RGYAL BO'I GO SAR KHRI 'DON MDZAD,

CHU BYI (1672) LO'I LO SAR SKABS NAS RIN CHEN RGYAN CHA

SPRAS PA'I SROL BTZUGS, DE YANG BOD RJE CHOS RGYAL SKU DUS KYI CHAS

GOS GZHI BYAS NAS GSER GA SOG RNA, SOG SGOR, RNA RGYANGS,

SHAL DKAR DMAR, TZI GOS, TZI BER, GTZUG ZHVA STE RIN CHEN

RGYAN SPRAS SU GRAGS PA SDE SRID SNGON RABS DAG GI DUS BZHIN

MDZAD, SDE DRUG MKHAN PO BLO BZANG DAR RGYAS, HAL HA SDE GZHUNG

@183 GI BLA MAR RDZONG BDA' MDZAD,

BAR KHAMS PHYOGS SU DPON MKHA' 'GRO DANG SGAR BA SKU NYER

'BREL BA BYAS TE, BOD KYI BSTAN SRID LA GNOD PA BYUNG STABS,

MTSO SNGON NAS DA LA'I HONG THA'I JIS DMAG DPON BYAS, DGA'

LDAN DAR RGYAS TSE DBANG RAB BRTAN SOGS KYI DPUNG DMAG BAR

KHAMS SU 'BYOR BA TZAM GYIS DGRA PHYOGS KYIS MGO SGUR, DMAG

DPUNG PHYIR LOG DA LA'I HONG THA'I JI 'KHOR BCAS GNAS TSUL ZHU

BAR LHA SAR BYON,

SHING STAG (1674) LOR MDO KHAMS RGYAL THANG PHYOGS SU

BOD GZHUNG SKU TSAB KYI BKA' MI BRTZI BA BYUNG STABS, AUL JO'I

THA'I JIS DMAG DPON DANG, DE'I ROGS PAR BKA' BRGYAD

NOR BU, MAS CHAGS PA DPUNG BCAS RDZONG BDA' MDZAD PA LTAR

SONG NAS DPUNG 'JUG TSA NAN BYAS, SHING YOS (1675) LO'I

NYES BSTUN GYI CHAD LAS BKAL,

ME 'BRUG (1676) LOR SDE SRID MTHU STOBS DGONGS ZHUS

KYIS ZUR BZHUGS MDZAD, RNAM RGYAL GRVA TSANG GI GNYER BA BLO BZANG

SBYIN PA SDE SRID DU BSKOS, ME SBRUL (1677) LO 'BA' CHOS

@184 SDE DGON LA PHOGS THOB SNGAR YOD THOG 'PHAR SNON MCHOD GZHIS

THEBS MCHOD GZHIS THAG BCAD,

PE CIN NAS GONG MA KHANG SHIS BANG CHEN PA MNGAGS TE, RGYA

NAG GI NANG BLON PHING SING WANG GI NGO LOG GIS NANG 'KHRUG BYUNG

@190 RAB NYI CHU RTA (1702) LOR RGYAL BA TSANGS DBYANGS RGYA MTSO

@192 BZANG RGYAL BO'I MTSAN GNAS RANG 'JOG THOG MTSO SNGON PHYOGS SU

KHAG GSUM, GUNG THANG LHA SDE DMAG GSAR MA, SKYA MGO, RONG

RU, TSA RU, TSA LUNG STE SDE BZHI, ZANGS DKAR KHAG GSUM

BCAS BSNAN NAS HUNG YON RDZONG (?) BTZUGS, AA MCHOG

KHAG GSUM NI GTZANG BKRA SHIS LHUN PO'AM, GZHIS KA RTZE'I THAG

NYE'I AA MCHOG CES PA'I SDE BA LAS, BOD CHOS RGYAL SKABS DMAG

TU 'ONGS PA DAG GI MI RGYUD YIN, SNGAR AA MCHOG RGYAL BO ZHES PA'I

MGO DPON ZHIG YOD LA, PHYIS SU DE'I MI RGYUD CHAD NAS AA MCHOG

SPRUL SKU'I LHA SDER GYUR, TSA RU, TSA LUNG SOGS NI MI RGYUD TSA KHOR

GTOGS, SNGAR COG TZE RGYAL BO'I MNGA' 'BANGS SU GTOGS,

@383 ZANGS DKAR KHAG GSUM NI STOD MNGA' RIS KYI ZANGS DKAR ZHES

PA'I YUL NAS 'ONGS PA'I MI RGYUD YIN LA, SNGON KHRO CHU'I MDA'

MKHAN TSANG GI RU SDE RED, 'DI DAG KYANG THANG BOD 'KHRUG PA'I

SKABS SU 'ONGS PA'I DMAG YIN NO, ,RDZONG GI LTE BA'I GRONG RDAL

NI KHYUNG MCHUR CHAGS YOD,

(DA DUNG KHA GYA TSO DRUG 'BO RA AA MCHOG ZAM TSA SHE'U TSANG

SOGS DANG, MTSO SNGON, REB GONG, DPAL RIS, BKA' MA

LOG SOGS KYI LO RGYUS 'BRI 'DUN YOD KYANG BREL DBANG GIS RE

ZHIG MTSAMS 'JOG DGOS BYUNG,)
